A given set of taxa can be related in a limited number of ways, but if each taxon is represented by multiple sequences, the number of possible topologies becomes very large. Topology weighting reduces this complexity by quantifying the contribution of each \u2018taxon topology\u2019 to the full tree. We describe our method for topology weighting by iterative sampling of sub-trees (<jats:italic>Twisst</jats:italic>), and test it on both simulated and real genomic data.
